<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grendel.html>grendel</a> (10563)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:grendel.html>grendel</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">grindel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">grindel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*grindil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grindilaz</i>. 
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***grens.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grens.html>grens</a> (1693)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed in the 16th century from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">grense</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">grenitse</i> and/or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:grenzen.html>Grenze</a></i>, both ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Polish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Polish">Old Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="zlw-opl">granica</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*granica</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grens.html>grens</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grenzen.html>grenzen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grens.html>grensje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>border, frontier</li>
<li>limit</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>gridiron</a> (64891)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Origin uncertain, perhaps related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">griddle</i>.  The ending <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> assimilated to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">iron</i>. <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(<span id="rfv-etymology-notice-en-"></span>Can this<sup class="plainlinks">(<a class="external text" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/w/index.php?title=Wiktionary:Etymology_scriptorium/2020/Augustamp;action=editamp;section=newamp;preload=Template:rfv-etymology/preloadamp;preloadtitle=%5B%5Bgridiron%23rfv-etymology-notice-en-%7cgridiron%5D%5D">+</a>)</sup> etymology be sourced?)</span>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Nyam%21.jpg/220px-Nyam%21.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Nyam%21.jpg/330px-Nyam%21.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Nyam%21.jpg/440px-Nyam%21.jpg 2x" data-file-width="700" data-file-height="525" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>A <a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>gridiron</a></div></div></div>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>gridiron</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gridirons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An instrument of torture on which people <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> secured before being burned by fire. <span class="defdate">[from 13th c.]</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1603</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michel_de_Montaigne" class="extiw" title="w:Michel de Montaigne"><a href = vnd.unilang:michel.html>Michel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:montaigne.html>Montaigne</a></a>,  chapter 32, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Florio" class="extiw" title="w:John Florio">John Florio</a>, transl., <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Essays_(Montaigne)" class="extiw" title="w:Essays (Montaigne)">The Essayes,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="or, Morall, Politike and Millitarie Discourses of Lo. Michaell de Montaigne, Knight of the Noble Order of St. Michaell, and One of the Gentlemen in Ordinary of the French King, Henry the Third His Chamber">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite>, book II, printed at London |  By <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Valentine_Simmes" class="extiw" title="w:Valentine Simmes"><a href = vnd.unilang:val.html>Val</a>[entine] Simmes</a> for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Edward Blount</a><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="dwelling in Paules churchyard">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/946730821">946730821</a></small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I know, there have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> found seely boores, who have rather endure to have their <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a> broiled upon a <b>Greedyron</b>, their <a href = vnd.unilang:fingers.html>fingers</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ends.html>ends</a> crusht and wrung with the lock of a Pistoll, their <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> all bloody to be thrust out of their heads with wringing and wresting of a cord about their foreheads, before they would so much as be ransomed.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>An iron rack or grate used for broiling meat and fish <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> coals. <span class="defdate">[from 14th c.]</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">iron</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">grid</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From resembling the shape of a <a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>gridiron</a> (a square rectilinear grid)
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>gridiron</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gridirons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any object resembling the rack or grate. <span class="defdate">[from 15th c.]</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b>,  Andrew Martin,  <cite>Underground Overground: A passenger's history of the Tube</cite>, Profile Books, →ISBN, page 55:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Just north of Farringdon station, and to the east of <a href = vnd.unilang:ray.html>Ray</a> Street, there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a wide cutting bounded by another of those brick walls nicely calculated to be just too high for you to see <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>. So prop your bike against it, and stand on the down-pointing pedal crank. You are <a href = vnd.unilang:looking.html>looking</a> at the <a href = vnd.unilang:ray.html>Ray</a> Street <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>Gridiron</a></b>, a spectacular bridge in a cutting that <a href = vnd.unilang:carries.html>carries</a> the Metropolitan, the supposed Underground, <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the Widened Lines (now Thameslink).</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An openwork frame on which vessels are placed for examination, cleaning, and repairs.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:theater.html>theater</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A raised framework from which lighting <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> suspended.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">American football</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The field on which American football <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> played. <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Zealand" class="extiw" title="w:New Zealand">New Zealand</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> American and Canadian football, particularly when used to distinguish from other <a href = vnd.unilang:codes.html>codes</a> of football.
<ul><li><b>1995</b> October 3, <a href = vnd.unilang:peter.html>Peter</a> O′Shea, <i>Sports: Out on the field</i>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Advocate" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Advocate">The Advocate</a></i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=2WQEAAAAMBAJamp;pg=PA54amp;dq=%22gridiron+player%22%7C%22gridiron+players%22+-intitle:%22%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=XuhuT5_QCNGImQXR25iVBgamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22gridiron%20player%22%7C%22gridiron%20players%22%20-intitle%3A%22%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">page 54</a>,
<dl><dd>He represented Australia in this year′s rugby tour of England and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> as well-known in Australia as any top <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>gridiron</a></b> player <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in the United States.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2001</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Langston_Hughes" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Langston Hughes">Langston Hughes</a>, Dolan Hubbard, <i>Jackie Robinson: First Negro in Big League Baseball: 1919—</i>, <i>The Collected Works of Langston Hughes, Volume 12: Works for Children and Young Adults</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=LLhfJ5rlgKECamp;pg=PA105amp;dq=%22gridiron+player%22%7C%22gridiron+players%22+-intitle:%22%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=XuhuT5_QCNGImQXR25iVBgamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22gridiron%20player%22%7C%22gridiron%20players%22%20-intitle%3A%22%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">page 106</a>,

<dl><dd>119 Yasser (1985) cites the famous US example of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>gridiron</a></b> player <a href = vnd.unilang:dick.html>Dick</a> Butkus of the Chicago <a href = vnd.unilang:bears.html>Bears</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">playing field for American football</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">football field</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">football, Canadian and American</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">North American football</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>gridiron</a> football</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">football</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">North American English</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">American football</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">football</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US English</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>gridiron</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">gridirons</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">gridironing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">gridironed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To mark or cover with lines; to crisscross.
<ul><li><b>1901</b>, Archibald John Little, <i>Mount <a href = vnd.unilang:omi.html>Omi</a> and Beyond: A Record of Travel on the Thibetan Border</i>, Cambridge University Press, 2010, Conclusion, p. 242, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.ca/books?id=4VxiopcUE6sCamp;printsec=frontcoverv=onepageamp;qamp;f=false">[1]</a>
<dl><dd>This basin of Szechuan (literally "Four <a href = vnd.unilang:streams.html>Streams</a>," but which, reading the character idiographically, I should be inclined to render as "<b>Gridironed</b> by <a href = vnd.unilang:streams.html>Streams</a>"), <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1923</b>, Maximilian P.E. Groszmann, <i>A Parent's Manual: Child Problems, Mental and Moral</i>, New York: Century, p. 74, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.ca/books?id=HzhJAAAAIAAJamp;q=%22gridironing%22amp;dq=%22gridironing%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ved=0ahUKEwjmg834ypPNAhUT3GMKHTdHAqYQ6AEI4gEwKA">[2]</a>
<dl><dd>Another logical method <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that of <b>gridironing</b> the field by a series of straight paths that are parallel to each other.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1924</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herman_Melville" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Herman Melville">Herman Melville</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Billy_Budd" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Billy Budd"><a href = vnd.unilang:billy.html>Billy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:budd.html>Budd</a></a></i>, London: Constable amp; Co., Chapter 8, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://gutenberg.net.au/ebooks06/0608511h.html">[3]</a>
<dl><dd>When <a href = vnd.unilang:billy.html>Billy</a> saw the culprit's naked back under the scourge <b>gridironed</b> with red welts, and worse <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> <a href = vnd.unilang:billy.html>Billy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> horrified.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1949</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lewis_Sinclair" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Lewis Sinclair"><a href = vnd.unilang:lewis.html>Lewis</a> Sinclair</a>, <i>The God-Seeker</i>, New York: Popular Library, Chapter 42, p. 227,
<dl><dd>His white back, <b>gridironed</b> with scars, <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> as soft as a <a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a>'s.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2012</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:janet.html>Janet</a> Wallach, <i>The Richest Woman in America: Hetty Green in the Gilded Age</i>, New York: Anchor Books, 2013, Chapter 8, p. 111, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.ca/books?id=oKvaLKx8rEgCamp;printsec=frontcoverv=onepageamp;qamp;f=false">[4]</a>
<dl><dd>Railways spanned the continent and <b>gridironed</b> the states.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Zealand" class="extiw" title="w:New Zealand">New Zealand</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To purchase <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> so that the remaining adjacent sections are <a href = vnd.unilang:smaller.html>smaller</a> than the minimum area purchasable as freehold, thus excluding potential freeholders.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:griep.html>griep</a> (6069)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">grippe</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">gripper</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to seize, snatch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*grīpan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grīpaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰreyb-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grab, grasp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijpen.html>grijpen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Grippe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flu</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">grippe</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:griet.html>griet</a> (3797)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> girl, (young or any) female, often derogatory: broad</li></ol>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:griet.html>griet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grieten.html>grieten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grietje.html>grietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<ol><li>short for <a href = vnd.unilang:margriet.html>margriet</a>, an apple variety</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>An euphemistic alteration of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in curse <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a>, to remove the blasphemous nature.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:griet.html>griet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>euphemism for <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a>, notable as an alternative for blasphemous cursing</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:griet.html>griet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grieten.html>grieten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grietje.html>grietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Rhombus_vulgaris" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Rhombus vulgaris"><i>Rhombus <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></i></a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:brill.html>brill</a> a fish species</li></ol>

***grievous.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grievous.html>grievous</a> (42219)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">grieve</i>, from the <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">greven</i>, from the <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">grever</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gravō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I burden</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Developed in the 13th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grievous.html>grievous</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:grievous.html>grievous</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:grievous.html>grievous</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Causing grief, pain or sorrow.
<ul><li><b>1883</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Louis_Stevenson" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Louis Stevenson">Robert <a href = vnd.unilang:louis.html>Louis</a> Stevenson</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Treasure_Island" class="extiw" title="w:Treasure Island">Treasure Island</a></i>
<dl><dd>As for the <a href = vnd.unilang:captain.html>captain</a>, his wounds <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grievous.html>grievous</a></b> indeed but not dangerous.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Serious, grave, dire or dangerous.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>See also Thesaurus:lamentable</li></ul>
</body>

***griffin.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:griffin.html>griffin</a> (6818)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">griffoun</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">griffon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gryphus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γρύψ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grúps</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Cotta_Greif_1839.jpg/220px-Cotta_Greif_1839.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="241" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Cotta_Greif_1839.jpg/330px-Cotta_Greif_1839.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Cotta_Greif_1839.jpg/440px-Cotta_Greif_1839.jpg 2x" data-file-width="726" data-file-height="794" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>a <a href = vnd.unilang:griffin.html>griffin</a> (1)</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:griffin.html>griffin</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:griffins.html>griffins</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A mythical beast having the body of a lion and the wings and head of an eagle.</li>
<li>A large vulture (<i>Gyps fulvus</i>) found in the mountainous parts of Southern Europe, North Africa, and Asia Minor, supposed to be the "eagle" of the Bible.</li>
<li>An English variety of apple.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/India" class="extiw" title="w:India">India</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> just arrived from Europe.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1842</b>,  <cite>The Asiatic journal and monthly register</cite>, volume 38, page 40:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Tables <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> laid out in the palace, profusely covered with wines and refreshments, in the European style; old hands and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:griffins.html>griffins</a></b>, fair sex and civilians, seemed all determined to enjoy themselves<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of H. Kingsley to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A cadet newly arrived in British India: <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> English, <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> Indian.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup></li>
<li>A watchful guardian, especially a duenna in charge of a young woman.</li></ol>
</body>

***grijs.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grijs.html>grijs</a> (5335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijs.html>grijs</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*grīs</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grīsaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijs.html>grijs</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijzer.html>grijzer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grijs.html>grijs</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">grijst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">grey</span>, grey-colored</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> referring to grey hair</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">old</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">weathered</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">tarnished</span>, affected by wear and tear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gozer.html>Gozer</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> ille <a href = vnd.unilang:plaat.html>plaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jantje.html>Jantje</a> Smitje <a href = vnd.unilang:helemaal.html>helemaal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grijs.html>grijs</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedraaid.html>gedraaid</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Dude, I wore that wicked record by <a href = vnd.unilang:jantje.html>Jantje</a> Smitje completely out.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>partially illegal</li></ol>

***gril.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gril.html>gril</a> (20788)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">grille</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cricket</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Grille</i>).  Perhaps the shift in sense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> due to a conflation of <a href = vnd.unilang:crickets.html>crickets</a> with earwigs, involving the popular myth of insects which crawl through the ears to lay eggs in the brain, altering a person's behaviour.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gril.html>gril</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grillen.html>grillen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gril.html>grilletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:caprice.html>caprice</a>, whim, impulse</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gristen.html>gristen</a> (117097)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gristen.html>gristen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention"> plural past indicative and subjunctive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grissen.html>grissen</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Exaggeration of an orthodox Protestant pronunciation of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:christen.html>christen</a></i>, <span class="IPA">/xrɪs.tən/</span>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Obsolete spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:christen.html>christen</a></i></span></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">Jesus <a href = vnd.unilang:freak.html>freak</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> botherer</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">pejorative for conservative Christians</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***groef.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:groef.html>groef</a> (20329)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:groeve.html>groeve</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">grove</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gruova</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grōbō</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groeve.html>groeve</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groef.html>groef</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groeven.html>groeven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groefje.html>groefje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>wrinkle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">woodwork, metalwork etc...</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a groove carved into an object or a joint between two pieces of wood (such as a tongue and groove joint)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groeven.html>groeven</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***groeien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:groeien.html>groeien</a> (2302)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">groeyen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gruoien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grōaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰreh₁-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grow, become green</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with English grow.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groeien.html>groeien</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to grow</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:groen.html>groen</a> (2146)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:groene.html>groene</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gruoni</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*grōnī</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grōniz</i>.
</p><p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">grön</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">gröön</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">grün</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:grien.html>grien</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">green</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">grøn</i>.

***groente.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:groente.html>groente</a> (8278)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groen.html>groen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-te</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groente.html>groente</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groenten.html>groenten</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groentes.html>groentes</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groentje.html>groentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">groentetje</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> collective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Vegetables.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A (type of) vegetable.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:groente.html>Groente</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> typically not used for a single piece of vegetable; instead that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> called <i>(<a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stuk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groente.html>groente</a></i>. However, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used as a countable noun in both the singular and plural for a particular type (species, genus, cultivar, etc.) of vegetable.</li>
<li>While <i>groentetje</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the regular form of the diminutive, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not often used, likely because of its more difficult, less smooth pronunciation. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:groentje.html>Groentje</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the commonly used dimunitive.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:groente.html>groente</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:plantkunde.html>plantkunde</a>)</span> <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:voeding.html>voeding</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:eetbaar.html>eetbare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:planten.html>planten</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:delen.html>delen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daarvan.html>daarvan</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:echter.html>echter</a> let <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a>! <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i>In Nederland at <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardappels.html>aardappels</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:groente.html>groente</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vlees.html>vlees</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd>
<dd><span style="color:0060ff;font-weight: bold;">▸</span> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:elke.html>Elke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:denderden.html>denderden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrachtwagens.html>vrachtwagens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:groente.html>groente</a></b>, fruit <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijn.html>wijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zuiden.html>Zuiden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:parijs.html>Parijs</a>.</i><sup id="cite_ref-Route_Nationale_7,_leuker_dan_de_Route_du_Soleil_4-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-Route_Nationale_7,_leuker_dan_de_Route_du_Soleil-4"> | 4 | </a></sup></dd></dl></li></ol>

***groep.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:groep.html>groep</a> (996)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">gruppo</i>, though possibly borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">groupe</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krop.html>krop</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groep.html>groep</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groepen.html>groepen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groepje.html>groepje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>group
<ul><li><b>1604</b>, Karel <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> Mander, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> schilder-boeck</i>, publ. by <a href = vnd.unilang:jacob.html>Jacob</a> Pietersz. <a href = vnd.unilang:wachter.html>Wachter</a> (print from 1618), page 112.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>Hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ſeer aerdich uytgebeeldt <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> grouwelijck Zee-onweder / daer oock <a href = vnd.unilang:noch.html>noch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ander.html>ander</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schepen.html>Schepen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> Schuyten vande <a href = vnd.unilang:felle.html>felle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:winden.html>winden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bevochten.html>bevochten</a> / ſeer <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> grooter aendacht ghedaen: ghelijck oock <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> eenen <b><a href = vnd.unilang:groep.html>groep</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:beelden.html>beelden</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> locht / in verſcheyden ghedaenten <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> quade gheeſten / <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:winden.html>Winden</a> blaſen / <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schip.html>Schip</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> raſende <a href = vnd.unilang:golven.html>golven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:riemen.html>riemen</a> crachtelijck wort geroeyt / <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beletten.html>beletten</a>.</span><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this quote)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>circuit in an electrical installation, protected by a circuit breaker</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In Belgium the word normally <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> the masculine gender. The feminine gender may still occur in formal Dutch from the Netherlands.
</p>

***groeten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:groeten.html>groeten</a> (1990)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:groeten.html>groeten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gruoten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grōtijaną</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grollen.html>grollen</a> (69765)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:grollen.html>grollen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to debase; lower; humiliate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">*<a href = vnd.unilang:grollen.html>grollen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gruljaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to yell; shout at</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰer-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grumble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">gellen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to shout</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, compare <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grillen.html>grillen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to shiver, shake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">grill</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to provoke</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">growl</i>.
</p>

***grond.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grond.html>grond</a> (727)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gront</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">grunt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grunduz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grond.html>grond</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gronden.html>gronden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grond.html>grondje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ground, dirt, soil</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> floor, ground
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grond.html>grond</a></b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">on the floor/ground</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>ground, <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a>, territory</li></ol>
